# Use 'L' for all Luclin models 'N' for all NGE models and '*' for all models.

# For robes and legging the Luclin attach point is Pelvis and the equivalent NGE point is 'legs'.

# for the /armorattach command these are the slot numbers just for the text commands:							
# 0-head 1-chest 2-shoulders 3-bracers 4-Hands 5-legs/pelvis 6-feet							
#							
# 1001+ are the unique ARMOR SLOT IDs: 							
# Each ID needs to be unique WITHIN a set. 							
# Every SLOT needs to be unique for a different model in the game.
